  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e76165d3-d79c-4b3f-8613-df0bb2a047e9'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer2213302493261861032">Indy Savage, cop's daughter, rock chick and used bookstore owner, has been in love with Lee Nightingale, once bad boy, now the man behind Nightingale Investigations, since she was five years old.   <span id="freeText2213302493261861032" style="display:none">Indy Savage, cop's daughter, rock chick and used bookstore owner, has been in love with Lee Nightingale, once bad boy, now the man behind Nightingale Investigations, since she was five years old. No matter what ingenious schemes Indy used to capture his attention, Lee never showed an interest and Indy finally gave up. Now Indy's employee, Rosie, has lost a bag of diamonds and bad guys are shooting at him. When Indy gets involved, Lee is forced to help. Complicating matters, Lee has decided he's interested, Indy's decided she's not. But she can't seem to keep Lee out of her life when she's repeatedly stun gunned, kidnapped and there are car bombs exploding (not to mention she's finding dead bodies).<br /><br />Indy's best bet is to solve the mystery of the diamonds before Lee. Lee's challenge is to keep Indy alive and, at the same time, win back her heart.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1107744-i-ve-read-almost-all-of-ka-s-backlist-at">I&#39;ve read almost all of KA&#39;s backlist at this point...except the Rock Chicks series. I avoided it because it just didn&#39;t seem like my style, but now I&#39;m wondering if it&#39;s worth going back and starting KA &quot;from the beginning&quot;? Do these books hold up/are all the crazy-good ratings justified, despite being her first novels ever written? (Especially when someone has already read most of her other stuff.)</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1107744'><a id="like_count_community_question_1107744" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/1107744?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">1 like</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F6538757-rock-chick">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/1107744-i-ve-read-almost-all-of-ka-s-backlist-at">3 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/1107744-i-ve-read-almost-all-of-ka-s-backlist-at">See all 3 answers</a>
</li>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/33763037-nikki"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1540068832i/33763037._UX100_CR0,20,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/33763037-nikki">Nikki</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I agree with Linda L. I actually came across the Unfinished Hero series first so Knight was my first. That series led me to plow through Dream Man bec<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I agree with Linda L. I actually came across the Unfinished Hero series first so Knight was my first. That series led me to plow through Dream Man because I already loved some of the men in them. Then I started on the Chaos series. But I decided to go back to the beginning to see what I may have missed out on because I've always loved Lee's character when he appears in the other books. <br /><br />Naturally, writing can build and develop over time, so earlier books may not be as compelling. There is a lot to love here, but there's also a lot of build up with sometimes no payoff. If you're reading this and just can't wait until they finally get that alone time all hot and heavy, prepare to be disappointed. It gets hot and heavy and then the shot may as well pan to a wall like in a chick flick. In later books, we would at least get one good payoff after a huge, sexual-tension-filled buildup. Some shorthand here and there after that is okay, but that part was just a letdown, and I don't read just for the naughty bits.<br /><br />So basically, after everything else that I LOVE, it's been a bit of a letdown for me.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer262382168" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7373899402856170964"><b>2 stars</b><br/><br/>I guess this is one of those books that everyone loved but me. <br/><br/>I tried! I really tried to love this book. Then I tried to like this book. Then I just tried to finish this book. Unfortunately, Indy, the heroine, ruined the story for me. <br/><br/>I'm honestly at a loss trying to express my sheer annoyance, disapointment, and frankly, total embarrassment with Indy's character. Not only was she flat out nuts, had one too many TSTL (to stupid to live) moments, and was beyond wishy washy; but, she was a</span>
  <span id="freeText7373899402856170964" style="display:none"><b>2 stars</b><br /><br />I guess this is one of those books that everyone loved but me. <br /><br />I tried! I really tried to love this book. Then I tried to like this book. Then I just tried to finish this book. Unfortunately, Indy, the heroine, ruined the story for me. <br /><br />I'm honestly at a loss trying to express my sheer annoyance, disapointment, and frankly, total embarrassment with Indy's character. Not only was she flat out nuts, had one too many TSTL (to stupid to live) moments, and was beyond wishy washy; but, she was also the stupidest heroine I've read to date. I mean, the girl needed a basic refresher course in 6th grade sexual education for heaven sakes! <br /><br />The only good that came from this book, in my opinion, was the amazing and sexy hero, Lee Nightingale. I loved his charcter and name! Other than that, I did not enjoy this story. I hope I'll have better luck with the rest of the series. <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>

<div id="review_1712409282" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1712409282" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1712409282?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1712409282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16406204944946827701"><b>This was my first <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> experience, and I am officially <u>confused</u></b>.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443782469ra/16410442.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let me explain.<br/><br/><b>1)</b> You are finally together with the man you've been in love with your entire life. Do you flirt with his colleagues and friends in front of him?<br/><br/>a) Hell to the no, why would I do that?<br/>b) Hell yeah, momma likes some action!<br/>c) N/A<br/><br/><b>2)</b> You've been shot at and kidnapped. Your badass boyfriend (who has ties with the police <i>and</i> the mob) asks you to let him handle the situation and refrain from doing something stupid</span>
  <span id="freeText16406204944946827701" style="display:none"><b>This was my first <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> experience, and I am officially <u>confused</u></b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443782469ra/16410442.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me explain.<br><br><b>1)</b> You are finally together with the man you've been in love with your entire life. Do you flirt with his colleagues and friends in front of him?<br><br>a) Hell to the no, why would I do that?<br>b) Hell yeah, momma likes some action!<br>c) N/A<br><br><b>2)</b> You've been shot at and kidnapped. Your badass boyfriend (who has ties with the police <i>and</i> the mob) asks you to let him handle the situation and refrain from doing something stupid because the guys you're dealing with are super dangerous (and creepy). You:<br><br>a) Do as he told because you don't want to die young<br>b) Do the exact opposite, attack assassins and get kidnapped again while you pretend to be a ninja because no man will tell you what to do (but at the same time when things get serious, you wait impatiently for him to come rescue you and clean up your mess)<br>c) N/A<br><br>If you answered at least one a) like me, then <b>Indy will <u>annoy</u> the crap out of you!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464724067ra/19269287.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My life had been simple a day ago. Work, coffee, rock 'n' roll. Now I was being shot at, dragged around by bad guys and propositioned by the love of my life who I had decided I didn't want anymore.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>That's what happens in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_" title="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a>! <b>Stolen diamonds, hitmen, icky and slightly insane crime lords</b> and Indy in the middle, because she was at the wrong place the wrong time. But this unfortunate situation brings her closer to Lee, the man she's been in love with since she was 5 years old and rejected her repeatedly, who has made up his mind and wants to be with her at all costs. And is also involved in this bizarre diamonds hunt. Indy tries to resist Lee's charms and solve the case on her own, because she is a Rock Chick and doesn't like staying behind. Even if that means discovering dead bodies, being kidnapped <i>three</i> times and endangering everyone near her.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I haven’t been avoiding you.” <br>“You’re lying. The last time we were both at dinner, you got up in the middle of Mom’s fajita presentation and said you forgot to feed your cat.”<br>“So?”<br>“You don’t have a cat.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>I really liked this book</b>, I can't deny that! It was <b>funny</b>, with a <b>generous dose of action and sexual tension</b>, and I would rate it higher if it wasn't this <b>long</b> and if Indy stopped acting like a 6 years old. Yes she was cool and strong-minded but man! there were times I wanted to throttle her! She argued for the sake of arguing and had the weird belief that being a Rock Chick means never listen to the voice of reason because this voice belongs to a man, a <b>hunk-a-licous</b> man I may say, who wants to protect you because you're <b>batshit crazy</b>! I listen to metal and enjoy a decent headbanging once in a while but I don't stun gun people in bar fights and I don't play detective when I'm not even sure what's at stake (besides my life, of course!).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432601499ra/14987019.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Setting aside Indy's shenanigans, I did enjoy the story! There were plenty of interesting and hilarious characters, and Lee had me drooling because <b>holy.hawt.alpha.male.alert</b>! He was <b>cocky</b> and <b>badass</b> and very, <i>very</i> <b>yummy</b>! And patient, anyone else would run away from Indy faster than Road Runner! Their scenes were loaded with <b>sizzling tension</b>, and I loved the fact that they had history together and knew each other so well. I would not mind spending the rest of my days in Lee's cabin, just saying!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I don’t get a taste of you soon, I’m givin’ up the search and takin’ you to my cabin in Grand Lake. No phones, no cell coverage, no buzzer. Anyone knocks on the door and I’m shooting them.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, I think I'll give <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> another shot, but only if I get some guarantee that I will not want to murder her female characters! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452724830ra/17733234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="16406204944946827701" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_247619735" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/247619735" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/247619735?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247619735" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17912919015186131255"> <b> Pure. Freaking. <i> Gold. </i></b>  LOVE LOVE LOVED this hilarious, romantic, action-packed book!!<br/><br/>This is probably the most all-out FUN book I've ever read! I mean, how can you not love a book about a smart, independent, sassy heroine and her Badass Extraordinaire hero getting together? huh? Its impossible not to I tell you. Impossible! :)<br/><br/>I cannot possibly gush enough. This book was BRILLIANT!! It had me flipping pages like mad, grinning endlessly and laughing and squeeing out-loud more times than I coul</span>
  <span id="freeText17912919015186131255" style="display:none"> <b> Pure. Freaking. <i> Gold. </i></b>  LOVE LOVE LOVED this hilarious, romantic, action-packed book!!<br><br>This is probably the most all-out FUN book I've ever read! I mean, how can you not love a book about a smart, independent, sassy heroine and her Badass Extraordinaire hero getting together? huh? Its impossible not to I tell you. Impossible! :)<br><br>I cannot possibly gush enough. This book was BRILLIANT!! It had me flipping pages like mad, grinning endlessly and laughing and squeeing out-loud more times than I could count!<br><br>Its insanely well-written. Kristen Ashley has an absolute gift with words. Her writing style is so effortless, you feel like you are right in the head of the main character.<br><br>The book is never boring, there is no stupidity from the characters, and the drama in the background compliments the character development of the story rather than complicates it. Its a delicate balance that Ms. Ashley has really perfected!<br><br>The story is about India "Indy" Savage and Liam "Lee" Nightingale. Indy's been in love with Lee since she was five. For reasons' you'll learn about, he couldn't admit he felt the same way until very recently. But they basically grew up together, then Lee went off to join the Army/Special Ops and went from badboy to Badass Extraordinaire and now runs his own detective agency. Fast track to present day, Indy's friend gets involved in some very shady business involving some illegally grown plants and million dollar diamonds, resulting in people shooting at them with guns and end up being helped out of the predicament by Lee... who of course uses this as the perfect stepping stone to finally get together with Indy.<br><br><i> "What was he playing at?<br>He told me.<br>And he told me bluntly.<br>“I do this thing for Rosie, you sleep with me"<br>I stared at him, open-mouthed and in stunned silence.<br>I did, of course, understand what he meant but he explained further.<br>"Not like last night, we'll both be naked and sexual acts will be performed."<br>My expression didn't change except maybe my mouth opened wider.<br>"I'll expect your participation."<br>Holy shit.<br>"Your avid participation."<br>Dear Lord in Heaven.<br>Eventually, I whispered, "You must be joking."<br>He shook his head and watched me.<br>I dropped my eyes, unable to hold his stare.<br>"I think I need more coffee,"" </i> <br><br>Oooooo Lee. Liam freaking Nightingale. I love you. There I said it. He's a wonderful hero - all delicious badass, uberly possessive, don't-fuck-with-me-or-my-woman, Alpha male. He is YUMMY!!<br><br><i> [conversation with her delightful gay neighbour]<br>"Girlie, he is fine. He's fine times twelve. He's the definition of fine."<br>"I've been in love with him since I was five," I told Tod. <br>"I'm in love with him now. I want to have his children, Tod told me." </i> <br><br>I loved that he doesn't play games, is open and honest about his feelings and thoughts even to the point of being cocky but never hides anything. What you see is what you get. Oh, and did I mention he's totally hot?<br><br><i> "Jesus," he buried his face in my neck. "There's nothin' better in the world than hearing you say my name when I'm inside you." He slid in deeper, filling me. "I've been waiting years to be right here." </i> <br><br>And Indy was feisty, fun-loving, sassy, takes-no-orders-and-won't-back-down-from-anything, funny, not at all annoying and totally lovable!<br><br>And I loved that they had known each other their whole lives instead of just meeting and hooking up. Its gave a familiarity to the characters - and made their fast relationship much more believable.<br><br><i> "I like that we have history and our kids will have a big family and share that history because there was never a time when their Mom and Dad weren't together." </i> ~Lee<br><br>This book is full of typical KA fun - there are kidnappings galore, car chases, steamy bedroom scenes, swoony moments, outright hilarious moments, drag queen performances, shoot-outs, explosions, a seriously epic food-fight, and of course, a wonderful love story. Also, we get introduced to a bunch of wonderful side-characters who will be heavily featured in the rest of the series :)<br><br>I absolutely ADORED this book!! and I recommend it to everybody and anybody! Run and get this book - you won't regret it!!<br><br>Here's how I see Lee and Indy:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380365032i/716862._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17912919015186131255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=swoonworthy-characters">swoonworthy-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=best-heroines">best-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=omg">omg</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=quick-witted">quick-witted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559954641" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8168415188598655046"><b>So, I’ve decided to bring this book with me to Thanksgiving dinner.</b><br/><br/>Why, you ask?<br/><br/>Well, that’s a silly question.<br/><br/>I mean, I have to have <i>something</i> to show good ol’ Aunt Deb when I tell her that my future husband is Lee Nightingale.<br/><br/><b>Duh.</b><br/><br/>Otherwise everyone will just think I’m crazy.<br/><br/>Which is ridiculous.<br/><br/><b>Clearly.</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_llt9njPv9H1qkyn24o1_500.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413216ra/813327.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_llt9njPv9H1qkyn24o1_500.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>But enough about Lee. I’ll get to him later…<br/><br/>*eyebrow waggle*<br/><br/>I want to talk to ya guys about Kristen Ashley. This is the first novel of her that I’ve read (we’ll celebrate later)… and it’s craz</span>
  <span id="freeText8168415188598655046" style="display:none"><b>So, I’ve decided to bring this book with me to Thanksgiving dinner.</b><br><br>Why, you ask?<br><br>Well, that’s a silly question.<br><br>I mean, I have to have <i>something</i> to show good ol’ Aunt Deb when I tell her that my future husband is Lee Nightingale.<br><br><b>Duh.</b><br><br>Otherwise everyone will just think I’m crazy.<br><br>Which is ridiculous.<br><br><b>Clearly.</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_llt9njPv9H1qkyn24o1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413216ra/813327.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_llt9njPv9H1qkyn24o1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But enough about Lee. I’ll get to him later…<br><br>*eyebrow waggle*<br><br>I want to talk to ya guys about Kristen Ashley. This is the first novel of her that I’ve read (we’ll celebrate later)… and it’s crazy because right away, her writing FLOORED me! She has such a signature writing style that I love! It’s witty; it’s snarky; it’s sexy. And she’s just so comfy with it, know what I mean? This is an author who completely <i>owns</i> what she does. <br><br>AND I LOVE THAT! <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_lpt85qZgCT1qc49r2o1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413216ra/813328.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lpt85qZgCT1qc49r2o1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>So onto the story…</b><br><br><i>Rock Chick</i> in a nutshell, is about a kickass girl, Indy Savage. <br><br>Indy owns a bookstore, and her brilliant coffee-maker-guy gets into trouble. Because well, he’s a pot (as in marijuana) seller. And <i>he</i> makes the mistake of selling to the wrong guy, who instead of paying coffee-maker-guy in cash, pays him in <b>diamonds</b>. That didn’t even belong to him in the first place.<br><br>Follow?<br><br>So because they don’t belong to him, coffee-maker-guy is now stuck with stolen diamonds. And one morning he shows up to work, at Indy’s bookstore, and they both get shot at… because they have stolen diamonds.<br><br>Now, Indy is the daughter of a cop. So she has plenty of people to call for help on this. But she knows there’s only really <b>one</b> man who can get the job done.<br><br>*BIG eyebrow waggle*<br><br>That’s right… she calls none other than THE Lee Nightingale. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/bac28c388b03a0aaa60e90c39fdb163c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413216i/813329._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo bac28c388b03a0aaa60e90c39fdb163c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the reason why I call him <i>the</i> Lee Nightingale is because that’s exactly how Indy thinks of him, as well. See, Indy has been in love with Lee since she was five. They grew up together. But he’s always been off limits.<br><br>Plus, he’s kind of scary. <b>As in jenny-get-your-gun scary.</b><br><br>So she calls him. And he, of course, helps her out. But he’s not just doing it be a good ol’ Samaritan. No no no… he’s doing it because he expects sexual favors in return. Which baffles the cruddola out of Indy, because well… Lee has always told her that he always saw her as the “little sister” type.<br><br>So now Indy’s getting shot at all of a sudden <i>and</i> the love of her life who she’s finally gotten over suddenly decides he wants her.<br><br>Aaaand…. I can’t tell you anymore because I’ll give everything away. ;)<br><br><b>So about the characters…</b><br><br>I loved every character in this book.<br><br><i>Every. Single. One.</i><br><br>I loved the stoner “Kevster” (his vocabulary is ha-ha-larious).<br>I loved Indy’s drag-queen neighbor.<br>And <i>laaaaaawd</i>, did I freaking LOVE cat-sitter Tex! (“Holy fuck, pandemonium at the gay bar!” &lt;-------- Best. Line. Ever.)<br><br>What was so awesome about the characters is that they’re all so eclectically <b>eccentric</b>. But they go together so well! Bravo, Kristen Ashley… bra-freakin-<i>vo</i>.<br><br><b>So about my review…</b><br><br>My review is this: this is book fantastic, and if you haven’t read it yet… I <i>really</i> don’t know what you’re doing sitting there reading this review. This book’s got everything: guns, car chases, hysterical one-liners, a kickass heroine, and one SEXY AS HELL alpha male &lt;----- Just remember he’s mine, okay? ;) <br><br><b>So…</b><br><br>***GO! GO! GO!***<br><br>Read <i>Rock Chick</i>, and let me know what you think!<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[P.S.<br><br>To those who <b>have</b> read it… HUGE HIGH FIVE! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1256561043?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘ by: </span>
      GR
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=annoying-mc">annoying-mc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1256561043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11872160453276696570"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429295103i/14566469._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Controlling asshole + TSTL heroine + plot nonsense + stereotypes everywhere = <u>I'm calling bullshit</u>.</b><br/><br/>For real, <b>this book takes the crappy romance at a whole new level</b> - I could be almost bewildered if I wasn't so pissed. <i>You know what?</i> I read the full book and I don't get it. I might write a full review when I calm down. Someday. In the meantime, I must introduce some facts to provide further information to explain my rating, because I do realize that I'm in a huge minority here.<br/><br/>Before I start, wh</span>
  <span id="freeText11872160453276696570" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429295103i/14566469._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Controlling asshole + TSTL heroine + plot nonsense + stereotypes everywhere = <u>I'm calling bullshit</u>.</b><br><br>For real, <b>this book takes the crappy romance at a whole new level</b> - I could be almost bewildered if I wasn't so pissed. <i>You know what?</i> I read the full book and I don't get it. I might write a full review when I calm down. Someday. In the meantime, I must introduce some facts to provide further information to explain my rating, because I do realize that I'm in a huge minority here.<br><br>Before I start, what you need to know is the fact that Indy knows Lee from her childhood and loved him almost always since, except for the 10 previous years. Why is it important? Why, because <b>it's used as the perfect excuse to explain that <u>there isn't ANY character development and/or relationship growth.</u></b> <br><br>➊ <b>Controlling asshole</b> : Okay OKAY I get it, I get it. Here's a handsome wild man, a tad mysterious, drop-dead sexy, who Indy loves since she's 5, who carries a gun and is protective, who's... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429541581i/14602481.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WHATEVER. I don't care about all these wonderful qualities, because :<br><br>1) <u>He is <b>repeatedly violent</b> in his moves</u> : he pushes her, catches her wrist, <i>"hook [her] around the back of the neck with enough force to send [her] slamming into him"</i>. Wow, how romantic. <br><br>2) <u>He wants to <b>control every one of her actions</b></u>, starting with their relationship : <i>"This is happening between you and me," he <b>threatened</b>."</i> Indeed Indy repeats several times that she is SCARED by him and his controlling behavior. What bothered me the most is the fact that the TSTL behavior of the heroine is used as an EXCUSE to explain Lee's reactions and to make the reader believe that it's okay. <b>Nope</b>. It's not okay to handcuff your girlfriend at the bed because you don't want her to go out. And it's certainly not okay to FORBID your girlfriend to wear what she wants to wear. Oh, but don't worry, Lee has an asshole as a friend who agrees with him. <br><br><i>"For what it's worth, I'm with Lee. If you were my woman, there's no fuckin' way I'd let you out of the house wearin' that."</i><br><br>YOU DON'T SAY?!<br><br>3) <u>He is a <b>jealous prick</b></u>. Now, a little jealousy can be great, but come on. Lee overreacts completely when Indy <i>talks</i> to another guy. <br><br>➋ <b>TSTL heroine</b> : basically, Indy is the stupid chick in scary movie. Yeah, you got it, the one we can't help but yell at to <b>STAY IN THE FUCKING HOUSE!</b> To sum up, she is kidnapped <i>3 times</i>, goes out <b>every time</b> someone tells her to stay hidden despite the really bad guys who constantly shot at her, decides to investigate while she obviously shouldn't (plus, she gives her real name to every dubious person she meets : who does that??). I know some readers found her kick-ass. I'm sorry but this girl? She isn't badass. No. When I think of her, here's how I picture Indy : <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429541581i/14602482.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What? She acts like she's 6 while she's 30. <br><br>Moreover, although in her inner monologues she complains about Lee's controlling behavior, <b>she always gave in. EVERY. FUCKING. TIME.</b><br><br>PS: I almost forgot to say that she is so fucking SPECIAL that she has 3 guys fighting for her. Yep. 3. <br><br>➌ <b>Plot nonsense</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429541581i/14602483._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know what? <b>I'm done</b>.<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_626519393" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/626519393" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/626519393?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11061688-rock-chick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=buddy-reads-are-the-best">buddy-reads-are-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=audible">audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=the-book-boy-is-mine">the-book-boy-is-mine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=jerk-of-my-dreams">jerk-of-my-dreams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=the-heart-wants-what-the">the-heart-wants-what-the</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=indie">indie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorite-secondary-characters">favorite-secondary-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer626519393" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8086924457735045943">This is the first Kristen Ashley (henceforth KA) book I ever read, and I LOVE it. <br/><br/>I read the rest of the ROCK CHICK books over the following week or two, and I loved them too, but I missed Lee and Indy. The whole time. Missed them. Now that I've reread it, I feel totally vindicated b/c they are as great as I remembered. <br/><br/>If you're new to KA, this is a good place to start. It follows her model, Indy is one of my favorite of KA's sassy, female MCs, and Lee is the archetypal seriously badass, ex-spe</span>
  <span id="freeText8086924457735045943" style="display:none">This is the first Kristen Ashley (henceforth KA) book I ever read, and I LOVE it. <br /><br />I read the rest of the ROCK CHICK books over the following week or two, and I loved them too, but I missed Lee and Indy. The whole time. Missed them. Now that I've reread it, I feel totally vindicated b/c they are as great as I remembered. <br /><br />If you're new to KA, this is a good place to start. It follows her model, Indy is one of my favorite of KA's sassy, female MCs, and Lee is the archetypal seriously badass, ex-special services, don't-worry-I-got-this guy. Their relationship is only made sweeter by the fact that Indy has loved Lee since she was five years old and he held her hand at her mother's funeral. BUH. (BUH &lt;-----means too cute for words.) <br /><br />So yeah. Really good HEA, no cliff-hanger, contemporary romance/romantic suspense. <br /><br />Also--I want a stun gun. <br /><br /><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br /><br /><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/626519860" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2)</a>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8086924457735045943" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_780144216" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/780144216" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/780144216?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-completed">series-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-modern">romance-modern</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-ipad">z-own-for-ipad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-playing-detective">c-playing-detective</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-lol-moments">i-lol-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-1st-book">series-1st-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-humor">genre-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-crime-or-mystery">genre-crime-or-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-obnoxious-females">c-obnoxious-females</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer780144216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8159587290190277455"><b>The first book in the Rock Chick series was highly amusing, but I don't think this book is for me...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389325573ra/8020877.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm kind of terrified of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> Fans... The author has this huge loyal following (which I was not aware of this until I started reading this) and they <i>love</i> these books... Like <i>REALLY LOVE</i> them... To the point that when I realized that this book wasn't (for me personally) living up to the hype, I got worried about how I would write this review.<br/><br/>With that in mind...<br/><b>Ms. Ashley, and her Adoring</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8159587290190277455" style="display:none"><b>The first book in the Rock Chick series was highly amusing, but I don't think this book is for me...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389325573ra/8020877.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm kind of terrified of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> Fans... The author has this huge loyal following (which I was not aware of this until I started reading this) and they <i>love</i> these books... Like <i>REALLY LOVE</i> them... To the point that when I realized that this book wasn't (for me personally) living up to the hype, I got worried about how I would write this review.<br><br>With that in mind...<br><b>Ms. Ashley, and her Adoring Fans, I want you to know the following:</b><br>1. I already plan to read some other series from the talented Ms. Ashley, and see if those work better for me.<br>2. I will always give my honest opinion in a book review, and I never expect the whole world to agree with me.<br>3. Maybe one day I'll try to read the rest of the series, and something will spark which was lacking this time.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389325573ra/8020878.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>THE AWESOME STUFF ABOUT THIS BOOK:</b><br>1. I am a total sucker for the "<i>girl crush grows up to become full blown love</i>" plot line *swoon*<br>2. Um... Lee Nightingale? Yes please!<br>3. Sassy heroine? Love that!<br>4. There were so many awesome secondary and tertiary characters.<br>5. The humor was great, even if it got down right silly at times.<br>6. Tex? Crazy cat man, coffee savant, looks like a serial killer? OMG yes.<br><br><b>THINGS WHICH WERE LESS THAN AWESOME:</b><br>1. You read the synopsis... there's a HUGE Mob plot in this book. Stolen diamonds, drugs, kidnappings, car chases, people got shot... So there should have been suspense, right? I didn't feel the suspense. <br>2. I was way not in love with India "Indy" Savage... She was a magnet for self-inflicted misfortune... It got old the <i>second</i> time she got kidnapped.<br>3. Indy was supposed to be thirty years old, but she had the emotional maturity of a nineteen year old, she was alarmingly sophomoric.<br>4. It was the mixture of immature humor and fumbled suspense which really wrecked the book for me... Consider a certain scene which began with someone being the target of a food fight (hee hee) and ended on the next page with that same person being the target of a car bomb (what?)... There were several other examples of this dichotomy, and it really diluted any threat of the Mob plot line being taken seriously.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386545972ra/7388174.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>HEAR ME OUT!</b><br>I really, really wanted to like this book!<br>I <u>am</u> a Rock Chick. I grew up listening to Mom's tapes of 70's rockers... I've tried to burst my own eardrums listening to Led Zeplin... I had my Grunge phase, my Metal phase, and yes... Even my Goth phase (lord help us all)... With the exception of Red Hot Chili Peppers (because I couldn't get tickets) I have been to <i>every single show</i> that Indy mentioned throughout this book... I am STILL one of the biggest TOOL fans you will ever meet in your life... I'd trade <u>all</u> my book boyfriends for Maynard James Keenan, and that just how it is. <br><b>So I say again... KA fans, don't hurt me...</b><br><br>And to all my friends and followers, <br>I'm not a hater. I will never hate on a book or an author for the sake of being negative. Nor will I ever lie about my feelings about a book to pander to a particular audience. And most importantly, I would never <i>ever</i> unfollow/unfriend or make nasty comments to a person simply because they don't like a book that I do. I'm classy like that, and I know that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> &amp; her fans are classy like that too.<br><br><b>
  <u>Some of My Favorite Moments:</u>
</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>He smiled.<br>He smiled The Smile.<br>Fuck, fuck, <i>fuck</i>.<br>Man, Lee could smile.<br><br>...I was never, never, never in a million years going to tell Lee Nightingale that I’d been in love with him since I was five and he sat next to me during my Mom’s memorial service and held my hand. I was never going to tell him it was a Bon Jovi-style shot through the heart when he told me he wasn’t interested in me because I was his little sister’s best friend. And I was never, never, never, ever going to tell him that something had changed in him and he scared the pants off me.<br><br><b>What was he playing at?<br>He told me.<br>And he told me bluntly.<br>“I do this thing for Rosie, you sleep with me.”<br>I stared at him, open-mouthed and in stunned silence.<br>I did, of course, understand what he meant but he explained further.<br>“Not like last night, we’ll both be naked and sexual acts will be performed.”<br>My expression didn’t change except maybe my mouth opened wider.<br>“I’ll expect your participation.”<br>Holy shit.<br>“Your avid participation.”<br>Dear Lord in Heaven.</b><br><br>Lee was not just a Bad Boy, a Badass or a Badass Extraordinaire, he was a fucking crazy man.<br><br>I figured it would be bad form to smack Lee in front of his mother.<br>And definitely strangulation was out.<br><br>I’d never replace Rosie at the espresso machine. He had a God-given talent, no joke. He was the Picasso of Coffee.<br><br>My life had been simple a day ago. Work, coffee, rock ‘n’ roll. Now I was being shot at, dragged around by bad guys and propositioned by the love of my life who I had decided I didn’t want anymore.<br><br>“Stop it, you’re crazy! One second you tell me to pack my bags, the next second you’re on me like white on rice.”<br>The backs of my knees hit the bed and we both went down, him on top of me, his lips on mine. “Gorgeous, give me ten minutes and I’ll be <i>in</i> you.”<br><br>“...Can’t be fun to be practically famous for fucking anything that breathes and being able to do so by expending the immense effort of just sending a smile their way. Then, later, you find yourself in a position where you’re serious about a woman who’s known you all your life and knows this fact <i>real</i> well and have to convince her you’re serious.”<br><br>They all wanted the facts, <i>all</i> the facts.<br>If I but breathed a word of what it actually was like to kiss Lee, be held by Lee, or, dear Lord, what Lee looked like naked, I might cause a riot, even a war. I might have to arm myself and fight them all back lest Lee be torn limb-from-limb.<br>It was for the better health of the female population and peace in the land that I kept my mouth shut.<br><br><b>“I gave him your excuses for missing dinner on Wednesday.”<br>“What were those?”<br>“You’d be with me and I’d be fucking your brains out.”</b><br><br>“He’s from Texas and he’s a drag queen. He has quick reflexes,”<br><br>“That was hardly the point.<br>Okay, it was <i>a</i> point, just not <i>the</i> point.<br>It was my longstanding theory that men missed <i>the</i> point on purpose.”<br><br>“He’s straight, he’s taken and if he turns, I have first dibs.”<br><br>“Holy fuck, pandemonium at the gay bar!” he yelled.<br><br><b>“Jesus,” he buried his face in my neck, “there’s nothin’ better in the world than hearin’ you say my name when I’m inside you.” He slid in deep, filling me. “I’ve been waitin’ years to be right here.”<br>Holy crap.<br>His mouth was at my ear.<br>“I could be on assignment, in a desert as hot as an oven, in a jungle as close as fuck and sometimes I’d get through it dreamin’ of you sayin’ my name like that.”<br>Holy crap, crap, crap.</b><br><br>I had to pull out the big guns.“There’ll be naked gratitude in it for you.”<br>Lee hesitated, but just for a moment.<br><br>“We gotta talk. Do you think Betty and Veronica here can keep an eye on these two?”<br>“I get to be Veronica,” Ally said instantly.<br>I turned to her. “Why do you get to be Veronica?”<br>I didn’t want to be Betty, Betty was a doormat. Veronica had attitude.<br>“I’m so Veronica,” Ally said in answer.<br><br>“Lee, you’re gonna have to get over this jealous-possessiveness thing.”<br>“Indy, you’re gonna have to get used to the fact that I’m the jealous-possessive type.”<br><br><i>Mace</i>? Who had a name like <i>Mace</i>? Where did these macho idiots come up with this shit?<br>“You got a guy named Mace?” I asked, I couldn’t help myself.<br>“His name’s Mason. Mason is a shit name. We call him Mace.”<br>That made sense.”<br><br>I discovered I loved stun guns, stun guns were righteous when they weren’t used on you.<br><br>“I don’t do hearts and flowers but I promise you won’t be disappointed.”<br>“You are so cocky.”<br>“Honey, I don’t give a fuck if you don’t believe it’s gonna be good between us. I know we’ll both enjoy me proving it to you.”<br><br>“Maybe we should have this conversation upstairs,” Lee suggested when he saw my attention turn to Eddie.<br>“Maybe we should have this conversation in an alternate universe where Alternate Indy gives a shit what Alternate Lee wants her to wear.”<br><br>“What’re you doing? Collecting the straight, super-macho Village People?”<br><br>“I’ll help you forget Nightingale,” Wilcox told me.<br>Okay, seriously, this guy was nuts. Even if he wasn’t a weird, creepy, icky, scary bad guy who killed people, there wasn’t a woman alive who would forget Liam Nightingale, especially if she’d seen him naked.<br><br>I wanted to run to him, throw my arms around him, do a lot of girlie, oh-my-god-I’m-glad-you’re-all-right and oh-my-god-I’m-glad-I’m-all-right stuff but his body language was not inviting that. This was badass Lee and hugs and cuddles were obviously not acceptable at this juncture. Therefore I kept my distance.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/423233955?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1609377-kara">Kara</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer423233955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12666170378345844915"><b>4.5 Rockin’ Stars!!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6dec715a-0d9a-4d7d-a5d0-d686a5563fdf_zps24ae5c21.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392588i/755744.jpg' alt=' photo 6dec715a-0d9a-4d7d-a5d0-d686a5563fdf_zps24ae5c21.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Indy Savage has been in love with her best friends brother, Lee, since she was five years old. Indy tried for years to get Lee’s attention, but you can only be rejected so many times. Indy is now 30, and the last 10 years or so, she has ignored Lee. It’s just easier that way. She see’s him at family events etc, but overall, she doesn’t spend time with him. A crazy night at her bookshop lands her delivered right to his door. With her friend and barista, Rosie, Indy gets s</span>
  <span id="freeText12666170378345844915" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Rockin’ Stars!!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6dec715a-0d9a-4d7d-a5d0-d686a5563fdf_zps24ae5c21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392588i/755744.jpg" alt=" photo 6dec715a-0d9a-4d7d-a5d0-d686a5563fdf_zps24ae5c21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Indy Savage has been in love with her best friends brother, Lee, since she was five years old. Indy tried for years to get Lee’s attention, but you can only be rejected so many times. Indy is now 30, and the last 10 years or so, she has ignored Lee. It’s just easier that way. She see’s him at family events etc, but overall, she doesn’t spend time with him. A crazy night at her bookshop lands her delivered right to his door. With her friend and barista, Rosie, Indy gets shot at. Rosie is in some trouble with some bad people. Indy’s bff, Ally, thinks it’s best they go to her brother Lee’s house, Lee isn’t home. Lee comes home early. And finds Indy in his bed. He has a special job, and he is willing to help Indy and Rosie... for a price...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I do this thing for Rosie, you sleep with me"<br>I stared at him, open-mouthed and in stunned silence.<br>I did, of course, understand what he meant but he explained further.<br>"Not like last night, we'll both be naked and sexual acts will be performed."<br>My expression didn't change except maybe my mouth opened wider.<br>"I'll expect your participation."<br>Holy shit.<br>"Your avid participation."<br>Dear Lord in Heaven.<br>Eventually, I whispered, "You must be joking."<br>He shook his head and watched me.<br>I dropped my eyes, unable to hold his stare.<br>"I think I need more coffee,"</blockquote>
</i><br>Lee knows what he wants. He wants Indy. He has wanted Indy for a long time. He had his reasons for pushing her away when they were younger, but now, this thing between them is happening. It takes a minute for them to ‘get together’, but when they do...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“Jesus," he buried his face in my neck. "There's nothin' better in the world than hearing you say my name when I'm inside you." He slid in deeper, filling me. "I've been waiting years to be right here.” </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Lovey%20for%20my%20books/GIFY5_zpsd39c44c8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392588ra/755745.gif" alt=" photo GIFY5_zpsd39c44c8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Indy gets into all kinds of trouble in this book. Getting kidnapped multiple times, using the stun gun often, and just being feisty and lol hilarious- she seriously cracked me up. She is one of the most fun and mischievous heroines I’ve ever read about. Indy and Ally together are even more of a hoot. She doesn’t take crap from anyone, even Lee.<br><br>Liam ‘Lee’ Nightingale is all kinds of hot, sexy, and alpha male. I wouldn’t expect anything less from KA. He is a bad ass. Possessive in the best way. <br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“Lee, you’re gonna have to get over this jealous-possessiveness thing.”<br>“Indy, you’re gonna have to get used to the fact that I’m the jealous-possessive type.” </i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>I just loved the two of them together. Even though Indy tried to fight it at first, they just fit together. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He’s good at this stuff.”<br>“What stuff?”<br>“Relationship stuff. He’s a natural. It’s weird, we’re new and we’re old. I can’t get my head around it.”<br>“He’s shit at relationship stuff. He’s only good at it because it’s you.”<br>“Sorry?”<br>“You’re shit at it too, but only because it was never him.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/cd2f4d7d-c4a2-4fea-bf16-4668c73fe6dd_zps1053fae0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392588i/755746.jpg" alt=" photo cd2f4d7d-c4a2-4fea-bf16-4668c73fe6dd_zps1053fae0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Indy and Lee were awesome, but holy hell there was a whole ensemble of FANTASTIC supporting characters! I am stoked for the rest of this series after meeting all these wonderfully unique and fun people. My absolute favorite was Tex. I hope he makes some cameo’s in the rest of the books because he was straight up awesome! Eddie, Ally, Hank, and many, many more great characters! <br><br>This was a great read, not my favorite KA book, but I still loved it! There was a TON of action, some mild suspense, romance, steam, humor and just straight up KA goodness. There were no boring parts, it was a fast paced book that didn’t drag at all. I am very much looking forward to continuing the Rock Chick series, especially since I know Eddie’s book is next! </span>
  <a data-text-id="12666170378345844915" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1296629857" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1296629857" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1296629857?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1296629857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16909576174121983695"><b>3.75 batshit crazy STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433238797i/15069549.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Honey, it's good you're gorgeous or you'd be a pain in the ass.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Finally. I've been meaning to get into KA's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/69392-rock-chick' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rock Chick series</a> for ages and suddenly the mood struck me. And here I am scrambling to write reviews, since I'm already on book three.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757-rock-chick' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rock Chick</a> is book one in the series and is one of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a>'s older works (published in 2008) and I would say you can see the difference. We get the usual overly descriptive style, a world filled to the brink with </span>
  <span id="freeText16909576174121983695" style="display:none"><b>3.75 batshit crazy STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433238797i/15069549.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Honey, it's good you're gorgeous or you'd be a pain in the ass.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Finally. I've been meaning to get into KA's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/69392-rock-chick" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick series</a> for ages and suddenly the mood struck me. And here I am scrambling to write reviews, since I'm already on book three.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757-rock-chick" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a> is book one in the series and is one of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a>'s older works (published in 2008) and I would say you can see the difference. We get the usual overly descriptive style, a world filled to the brink with detail, crazy stuff happening, slightly annoying heroines and bad-ass alpha males. But the writing is not as refined as it is in her older books. But to be honest I didn't care much. If there is one thing Ms. Ashley always accomplishes it is sucking me into her world and not letting me go until the end.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Rule Number One in the India Savage Life Code: When in doubt or possible trouble, lie. ”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>The story!</i><br><br><b>India Savage</b> also known as 'Indy' is a used book shop owner, tough girl, redhead and a rock chick. She has been in love with <b>Lee Nightingale</b> since she was five years old when he was holding her hand during her mother's funeral. For the better part of her teenage years, Indy tried to get together with Lee, who also happens to be her best friends brother. She was very obvious and forward about it. That is until she was 20 and Lee told her in no uncertain terms that he viewed her as his little sister and doesn't want to be with her. So for the last ten years she has kept her distance and even actively avoided the love of her life.<br><br>What the rock chick doesn't know is that Lee has always had a thing for her as well. But the circumstances were never right and he felt the need to stay away. That is until things changed and he found Indy sleeping in his bed after being in hiding from...bad people who are looking for some diamonds. <br><br>That's where the patented KA-CRAZY comes into play. One of Indy's employees, her coffee guru gets himself into a bind and being who she is Indy gets stuck in the middle. Luckily Lee is some sort of PI/fixer/badass/scary guy, who is feared by Denver's criminal underworld.<br><br>And Lee is quick enough to use the position to his advantage...if only Indy and his crazy sister Ally weren't prone to look for danger and trouble, his life would be a whole lot easier. All kinds of drama and over the top shenanigans ensue!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Your grandmother used to say that you were two souls separated in heaven. She mainly meant you were both trouble and deserved each other.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I have to say, I'm not 100% sold on Lee and Indy as a couple. They have this amazing and complicated history, but I didn't get that warm and fuzzy feeling KA couples usually evoke in me. I'm pretty sure it's because of all the drama. There rarely was a quiet and peaceful moment for them to really convince me. <br><br>But then again all the drama is what makes this book so unbelievably hilarious and addictive. It's filled with strange characters and lovable things, I just couldn't put it down.<br><br>Sometimes it takes me a week to finish one small novella, but a full length KA novel with 500 or 600 pages doesn't face me AT ALL. Read it within a day. That's how addicted I am and that's also the way these stories completely captivate my time and mind. It's easy content, fluidly written and magically predictable. <br><br>I'm thinking the Rock Chick series is a bit of an acquired taste. KA on steroids if you will. Everything you know from her other books (if you have read them) is double crazy. There are car bombs on every turn, people getting kidnapped, being shot at is a question of 'when' and not 'if' and the chicks have a knack for ignoring male advice. And let me tell you, it's good advice. But do they listen? Nope. Where would be the fun in that?<br><br>Crazy ride. Amazing reading times all around.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/296564736?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer296564736" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3257285803418632066"><br/><b>Re-read Review - August 19-21, 2013</b><br/><br/>You know, I've got so much going on in my life. Most of its great, but some not so great, so I decided I need to surround myself with some totally kickass women and hot, alpha males... So here I am doing a Rock Chick re-read! And I'm. In. Heaven!<br/><br/>Spending time with Indy, Lee, Ally...the entire cast and crew...exactly what I need. I've been giggling my butt off and loving every minute. I'm bumping my rating up to 5 stars because Rock Chick deserves nothing less!<br/><br/><b>O</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3257285803418632066" style="display:none"><br /><b>Re-read Review - August 19-21, 2013</b><br /><br />You know, I've got so much going on in my life. Most of its great, but some not so great, so I decided I need to surround myself with some totally kickass women and hot, alpha males... So here I am doing a Rock Chick re-read! And I'm. In. Heaven!<br /><br />Spending time with Indy, Lee, Ally...the entire cast and crew...exactly what I need. I've been giggling my butt off and loving every minute. I'm bumping my rating up to 5 stars because Rock Chick deserves nothing less!<br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br /><br />Indy Savage had been crushing on Lee Nightingale since she was five years old, but time and time again she’d thrown herself at him only to be shot down. The final and most humiliating rebuff came ten years ago when Lee told Indy that she was like a sister to him, and from that time on Indy did all she could do to avoid him. But when Indy’s friend and employee, Rosie, becomes the target of some very bad guys, and Indy gets dragged into it, hard-ass, won’t-take-no-for-an-answer, private investigator Lee makes sure that Indy’s days of avoiding him are over, once and for all.<br /><br /><i>Rock Chick</i> is funny, fast paced, sexy as all get out… exactly what I’ve come to expect from a Kristen Ashley story. Macho, hot, obnoxiously über alpha men and strong, independent, but loving and compassionate women pulled me in and kept me coming back for more. Lee and Indy make a great couple, and the supporting cast of friends and family kept me up until the wee hours of the morning, laughing out loud, fanning myself, and hoping it would never end.<br /><br />Such a great start to the <i>Rock Chick</i> series!<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492-kristen-ashley-addict-s-support-group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3257285803418632066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13584252281457144762"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*1.5 stars*<br/><br/><b>DNF at 50% (7 hours of listening). I give 1 star for the book plus an additional 1/2 star for the narration, which was actually pretty good.</b><br/><br/><i>If you are a hard-core, die-hard Kristen Ashley fan, look the other way! Shield your eyes from this review because, I promise you, it will only make you mad!</i><br/><br/>I honestly don't get the appeal of KA. This is my 4th book from her and they ALL feel the SAME! The SAME! Those staccato sentences, the way the heroines are always wrong and figure out that th</span>
  <span id="freeText13584252281457144762" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*1.5 stars*<br><br><b>DNF at 50% (7 hours of listening). I give 1 star for the book plus an additional 1/2 star for the narration, which was actually pretty good.</b><br><br><i>If you are a hard-core, die-hard Kristen Ashley fan, look the other way! Shield your eyes from this review because, I promise you, it will only make you mad!</i><br><br>I honestly don't get the appeal of KA. This is my 4th book from her and they ALL feel the SAME! The SAME! Those staccato sentences, the way the heroines are always wrong and figure out that the man was right all along, the helpless females... I actually think that her books have turned me off from "alpha males" for a long time. <br><br>Aside from the recycled plot, my biggest issue with this was Indy. I haven't met a heroine that personified "Too Stupid To Live" so perfectly in... maybe ever. How many times can a person get kidnapped? How many times can someone run into danger all for some coffee-weilding acquaintance? How many times can someone try to "leave the cops out of it" because she wants to handle it on her own? I just can't any more...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412775079i/11421302.jpg" width="300" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wasn't even interested enough to see how Indy and Lee got on as a couple. And I can't stand how KA leaves in so many mundane details. This book was hours/100 pages too long. Just endless boring scenes... <br><br>I'm going to have to wait a couple of years before attempting another book by this author. I risk dismemberment by her fans and disownment from my friends who love her work every time I try to read another one of her stories. <br><br>Sorry, guys. </span>
