<div id="review_416700490" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/416700490" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416700490?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/21802497-rock-chick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=top-audios">top-audios</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=best-of-the-bestest">best-of-the-bestest</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416700490" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15773761481190487886">Loved it...AGAIN!!<br/><br/>I think I'm going to have to do a KA marathon now. Once you start, you can't stop at just one.<br/><br/>************<br/><br/><b>The Rock Chick series is my happy place</b><br/><br/>I can’t believe I have never reviewed <i>Rock Chick</i>. This is by far one of my favourite books EVER!! <i>Rock Chick</i> is my go-to book when I need a pick me up. It’s funny, sweet, steamy and has one of the best alpha bossy heroes around. <br/><br/>In my everyday life, many things will trigger my need for a re-read. Someone mentions cashews and I automati</span>
  <span id="freeText15773761481190487886" style="display:none">Loved it...AGAIN!!<br><br>I think I'm going to have to do a KA marathon now. Once you start, you can't stop at just one.<br><br>************<br><br><b>The Rock Chick series is my happy place</b><br><br>I can’t believe I have never reviewed <i>Rock Chick</i>. This is by far one of my favourite books EVER!! <i>Rock Chick</i> is my go-to book when I need a pick me up. It’s funny, sweet, steamy and has one of the best alpha bossy heroes around. <br><br>In my everyday life, many things will trigger my need for a re-read. Someone mentions cashews and I automatically think of Indy’s kickass parties where she goes all out and even has cashews (WoW!). I’m feeling a bit sluggish and waiting for my coffee to brew, I think about trying the cup under the spout thing that Indy does (I’ve never attempted it mind you because I’m bound to stuff it up and spill coffee everywhere). It’s a Friday night and I’ve got no plans…why not live vicariously through Indy and be a <i>Rock Chick</i> for the night. I even hear Pearl Jam on the radio and it makes me chuckle that Indy stresses she’ll die before seeing Eddie Vedder in concert…which then gives me a bit of a buzz because I have (Ha Ha, I’m one-upping a book character). These are just some of the reasons why I keep going back again and again and again.<br><br>I’m not going to go too much into the story because there are heaps of reviews out there already. Obviously, I bloody love it. It’s bust a gut laughing, funny. There are sweet times that you can’t help but feel mushy, gushy over Lee. I love all the additional characters we meet in Indy’s adventures but special mention must go to Tex, Mr Kumar, The Kevster, Todd and Stevie, Duke and Brodie. You can’t help but grimace every time Coxy and his idiots show their faces, or when Dawn, Lee’s receptionist, swings her hips trying to tempt and seduce. By far, the best characters introduced...<i>The Hot Bunch</i>...Eddie, Mace, Vance and Hank.<br><br>I have read a few reviews talking about the way Lee treats Indy. There was concern that he mishandled her. Yes, he probably was a little forceful but I looked at it a little differently. Both Lee and Indy grew up together with all the banter, pranking and teasing that comes with being part of a family. No, they aren’t brother and sister (Ewww). It came across pretty clearly though that they feel comfortable to roughhouse, boss around and disobey each other. I never felt disgusted or sickened by it. I did…shake my head and make a tut, tut sound when Lee took things too far, or Indy disregarded Lee's well-meaning protection,but that was the Mum in me coming out.<br><br>Now…this narrator is the reason why I am now a fan of audio books. Sussanah Jones is AWESOME!! I love the way she changes her voice for characters. She’s very easy to listen to and understand. If you’re thinking about testing the waters with an audio book, it’s definitely worth checking out one of the books in this series.<br><br>To buy <i>Rock Chick</i> from Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2bX7BQ0">http://amzn.to/2bX7BQ0</a><br><br><b>I’m an Aussie chick who loves to read and review romance, drink coffee, be a <i>Style Setter</i> and stalk David Gandy. To see more of my reviews, fashion, food and pervathons -</b><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447925695i/17069306.jpg" width="170" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15773761481190487886" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

And I really tried :/<br/>But maybe it’s just one of the books everyone loves but me =[<br/><br/><i>All I was reading was this:</i><br/><br/><a href='http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9653897695/' title='blah von leonetta786 bei Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText181901259114049550" style="display:none"><b>*´¨)<br>¸.· ´¸.·*´¨) ¸.·*¨)<br>(¸.·´ (¸¸.·1 Stars</b><br><br>DNF after 45%<br><br>This book has 14,189 ratings and the average rating is 4.26 Stars! <b> 4.26!!!! </b> <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9220386805/" title="x von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869400.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="x" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t get it?? Am I weird for not liking it? Because I don’t think there was much to like. And I really tried :/<br>But maybe it’s just one of the books everyone loves but me =[<br><br><i>All I was reading was this:</i><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9653897695/" title="blah von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432682i/869401.jpg" width="248" height="320" alt="blah" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><u> <b> What I liked: </b> </u><br><br>► There were some funny parts^^ <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9441717703/" title="ha von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432682i/869402.jpg" width="240" height="165" alt="ha" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sadly that’s also the only good point I have :/<br><br><br><br><u> <b> What I didn't like: </b> </u> <i> This is going to be longer o.o</i><br><br> ►<u>Annoying characters:</u> <i>Was there any sane person in this book?? </i> <br><br><br>►<b>1)</b>Indy: <br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9387029276/" title="g von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869403.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="g" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>God, that girl needs a realty check, TSTL!! <br> The bad guys are after her. Does she care about the danger? No. Does she care about putting her friend in its way? No. -.-<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9654126499/" title="no von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869404.gif" width="500" height="270" alt="no" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Not to mention her “brilliant investigation skills”<i>*insert sarcasm*</i>. Which consider of driving somewhere and waiting for something to happen. She should have left this part to Lee or the police :/<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9627851345/" title="s von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869405.gif" width="500" height="291" alt="s" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But the thing about Indy that totally got on my nerves was her childish behavior. Indy is 30 and doesn't act like it. More like 13. So being stuck in here head was not a pleasant experience :D<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9313990711/" title="ö von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869406.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="ö" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>►<b>2)</b> Ally: <br><br>Most times I thought she was Indy Nr.2.<br> <br><i>Crazy Indy + Crazy Ally= </i><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9669398861/" title="cray von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869407.gif" width="500" height="375" alt="cray" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It might have been nice if Ally would be less like Indy. Honestly I don’t know how those two were able to keep out of trouble for so long...<br><br><br>►<b>3)</b> Lee: <br><br>The only character I actually liked at the beginning. He reminds me a lot of Hawke from Mystery Man. <br>The annoying thing about him was that we don’t know much about him. Yeah, he is a badass private investigator but if somebody asks about how he did something the answer is always: “He has his ways.”. I think this was meant to make him appear more mysterious but it actually just annoyed me. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9384257725/" title="w von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869408.gif" width="500" height="228" alt="w" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>►<b>4)</b> The Villain/Coxy:<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9316776170/" title="y von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869409.gif" width="500" height="215" alt="y" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What the hell is wrong with this guy??? Seriously needs to work on his image!*eye-rolling*<br><br>And one of his his mean “minion” was called Teddy.... way to kill the bad guy image XD<br><br><br>►<b>5)</b> Rosie: <i>First of all horrible name :D [Btw Rosie is a guy]</i><br><br>I like coffee. But is this reason enough for someone to go around and risk your life? Well, maybe yes. <br><br> <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9685689847/" title="cof von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869410.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="cof" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But it’s not about the coffee.(and all those coffee-god references started to get on my nerves) It’s about a guy that makes good coffee and which Indy doesn’t even really know.<br>I don’t know if he’s an important character or not. But he seems more like the explanation for the How-did-Indy-get-into-this-shit-question. <br><br><br><br><br>►<u>Plot</u>:<br><br>It dragged and dragged and dragged... I didn’t have any interest in the story. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9368387285/" title="ö von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869411.gif" width="500" height="215" alt="ö" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>______________________________________________________</b><br><br><i> So to sum it up: I didn’t care about the story nor did I like the characters. There are more things I didn't like but I think that's enough to explain why this book wasn't for me.</i><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/98072845@N05/9152824528/" title="q von leonetta786 bei Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432682ra/869412.gif" width="500" height="207" alt="q" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1756095666" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1756095666" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1756095666?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11061688-rock-chick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen">kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1756095666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2734528761265801192"><b> 3.5 stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Your grandmother used to say that you were two souls separated in heaven. She mainly meant you were both trouble and deserved each other.” </i> </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474340332i/20583770._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Rock Chick is the story of Indy and Lee. The two grew up together, always getting into shenanigans amongst Lee's siblings. But after being turned down one too many times by Lee, Indy has spent the last few years avoiding him.<br/><br/>Indy owns a bookstore/coffee shop and her best barista has brought chaos down on Indy's life involving diamonds, bad guys</span>
  <span id="freeText2734528761265801192" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “Your grandmother used to say that you were two souls separated in heaven. She mainly meant you were both trouble and deserved each other.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474340332i/20583770._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rock Chick is the story of Indy and Lee. The two grew up together, always getting into shenanigans amongst Lee's siblings. But after being turned down one too many times by Lee, Indy has spent the last few years avoiding him.<br><br>Indy owns a bookstore/coffee shop and her best barista has brought chaos down on Indy's life involving diamonds, bad guys and pot. Indy ends up needing Lee to help her, and Lee decides it's finally time she stopped avoiding him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456556813i/18248686.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> “So, now you’re getting shot at, you’re gonna leave me?”<br>“Girlie, I’m from Texas. We shoot at each other to say good morning.” </i> </b><br><br>I have to say I went into this with low expectations and enjoyed it a lot more than I thought I would. There are so many mixed reviews out there on this book, and these characters make appearances in other Ashley books so I knew it was worth a read. Many parts I was literally laughing out loud. But I can totally see how this book isn't for everyone.<br><br>I loved Indy as a character, such a free spirit and a cool gal. Lee was a little bit too........ alpha for me? To the point of his aggressiveness rubbed me the wrong way. But like I said, there were so many moments when I laughed while reading this book, I really enjoyed it overall and I am glad to see where Kristen Ashley got her start.<br><br><b> <i> “You want to marry me?”<br>“No. I’m gonna marry you.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455783307i/18148833._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2734528761265801192" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2121935914" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2121935914" />
    <a title="Kelly (and the Book Boar)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar"><img alt="Kelly (and the Book Boar)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530646317p2/11183856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2121935914?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly (and the Book Boar)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly (and the Book Boar)" href="/user/show/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar">Kelly (and the Book Boar)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar?shelf=everyone-loved-it-but-me">everyone-loved-it-but-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar?shelf=liburrrrrry-book">liburrrrrry-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar?shelf=blue-ballin">blue-ballin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar?shelf=hide-the-salami">hide-the-salami</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11183856-kelly-and-the-book-boar?shelf=i-need-a-12-step-program">i-need-a-12-step-program</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2121935914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9975716686408827624">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/>2.5 Stars<br/><br/>Indy has been in love with her best friend’s brother Lee ever since she was a wee little girl. When she was a teenager she threw herself at him (pretty much literally) for the last time. That’s when he told her she was like a sister to him. For the past decade, Indy has avoided Lee as much possible, but has never fully been able to due to their families' combined celebrations of birthdays/holidays/generic Sunday backyard BBQs,</span>
  <span id="freeText9975716686408827624" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>2.5 Stars<br><br>Indy has been in love with her best friend’s brother Lee ever since she was a wee little girl. When she was a teenager she threw herself at him (pretty much literally) for the last time. That’s when he told her she was like a sister to him. For the past decade, Indy has avoided Lee as much possible, but has never fully been able to due to their families' combined celebrations of birthdays/holidays/generic Sunday backyard BBQs, etc. When Indy finds herself in a real pickle featuring one of her employees (who just happens to be everyone in town’s favorite coffee guru) and a bag of diamonds, Lee plants himself firmly in her life. She also finds out when it comes to how he used to only view her in a “sisterly” manner, that . . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“That was then, this is now.”</i>
</b> <br><br>This had soooooo much potential. If you’re like me and have suffered through eleventy thousand Stephanie Plum stories, but can’t quit because they are your crack, you would have probably been all giggly schoolgirl upon starting this one too. Basically, Indy is a moron just like Stephanie. She gets kidnapped and blown up and shot at, etc., etc., etc. The difference here? SHE BANGS RANGER. Now, it takes a while to get there, but Lee is totally Ranger and they totally bang. (And you can just go ahead and spare me if you even are thinking of getting pissy and saying this isn’t like the Evanovich series because Kristen Ashley has in her mothereffing BIO that Evanovich is one of her influences.) So what went wrong?????<br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505498693ra/23930325.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ashley should have taken a bit more inspiration from Evanovich and realized that there was not enough story here for 400+ pages. I can get over the <i>very</i> loose “Rock Chick” gimmick – seriously girlfriend listened to rock music, wore denim miniskirts, bangles and big belt buckles and had a claim to fame of getting a little handsy with a guitar hero . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505498693ra/23930326.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To say the “Rock Chick” moniker was a bit of a stretch is the understatement of the year. Oh, and let’s talk about those clothes . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505498693ra/23930327.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Good Christ, I don’t need a description of every godblasted outfit the woman wore each day. There’s an old saying: “the devil’s in the details.” If that’s true, then Old Scratch must’ve had a front row seat during the writing of this one.<br><br>Some of you are probably asking why didn’t I just cut bait and DNF instead of letting it annoy the shit out of me for nearly three days? Well, because (1) KA really triggered the ol’ sploosh zone for me with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1538647926?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener"> one of her previous offerings</a>, (2) this one had some of the aforementioned things going for it as well as having a pretty LOL-able bad guy . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505498693ra/23930328.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Think I’m kidding????<br><br><b>
  <i>“He was short, had to be in his fifties and had jet-black hair with white at each temple. He looked like what I would guess a young Grandpa Munster would look like, except a lot more creepy and definitely scary, but not in a comic way.”</i>
</b><br><br>(3) It made me chuckle a few times. Not only because Indy was a loveable idiot, but also because of stuff like this . . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“Wear sexy panties tonight,” he said against my mouth. “I don’t have any other options except commando.” Lee’s arm tightened spasmodically right before he murmured, “Christ.”</i>
</b><br> <br>Not to mention (4) I was not blessed with the ability to not finish something. Mainly because . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505498693ra/23930329.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It probably goes without saying that I won’t be continuing on with this series. I’m sure that won’t hurt Kristen Ashley’s feelings one little bit since she has a mass of fangirls. Seriously, I don’t know how y’all do it. I get that these are self-pubbed, but for Jeebus' sake at some point you have to . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505498693ra/23930330.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I can't imagine the eye twitch I would develop if I managed to get through SEVEN more (FFS!) of these things.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9975716686408827624" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1488176305" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1488176305" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1488176305?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=book-boyfriend-material">book-boyfriend-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=adorable-alphas">adorable-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=cotton-candy">cotton-candy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1488176305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17487667573144310866">The Rock Chick series Buddy Read with some fellow hard core KA fans at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddies Books and Baubles</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287575i/17673738._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='393' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After a binge of emotional KA reads this is exactly the shift I needed. Yes at times it is ridiculous and over the top but I was having so much fun that I didn’t care at all and it made it even that more enjoyable.<br/><br/>First there aren’t a lot of books out there where there are a great girl friendships happening but KA does better than most. Indy and Ally have been friends forever, they are practically sis</span>
  <span id="freeText17487667573144310866" style="display:none">The Rock Chick series Buddy Read with some fellow hard core KA fans at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287575i/17673738._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="393" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a binge of emotional KA reads this is exactly the shift I needed. Yes at times it is ridiculous and over the top but I was having so much fun that I didn’t care at all and it made it even that more enjoyable.<br><br>First there aren’t a lot of books out there where there are a great girl friendships happening but KA does better than most. Indy and Ally have been friends forever, they are practically sisters and if Ally had her way they would be sisters by marriage but her stupid brothers didn’t fall into that trap just yet. <b>I love the girl friendship and banter between these two and how much trouble they got in together.</b> Yeah sure it is a little out there at times but I love how much they would do to protect the other.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452287575ra/17673739.gif" width="400" height="221" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Second there is just Indy on her own. She is still a wild child even though she is about thirty now and she has a very peculiar way of looking at the world. It is so entertaining and laugh out loud funny that I can’t pick out which of her crazy freak-outs or commentary were the funniest.<br><blockquote>“Late? We can’t be late! Dad loves you, Lee, but he’s not exactly jumping for joy that we’re together. We can’t be late the first time we go home for a barbeque!”<br>Lee’s face changed and his eyes became warm. “Are we together?”<br>Oh crap. I started thinking fast. “We’re not not together.”<br>“I’m not entirely certain what to do with that.” <br>I explained, <b>“We’re not exactly together and were not not together. We’re in together limbo. We’re test driving together to see if we want to buy it.”</b><br><br>And <br><br><i>“They’re on a Lee and Indy Sex Watch.” <br>“Come again?” <br><b>“They want to know when we’ve done it.” Silence. I went on, “If we don’t do it soon, they might force us to at gunpoint.” </b><br>“Christ.” <br>“I know. No pressure though. I told them we’re taking it slow.”<br>“You have to report in?” he asked.<br> “I kind of feel obliged,” I admitted. <br>“How’s that?” <br>I didn’t want to tell him I’d recruited them both for Lee Maneuvers in the past, so I said, “Never mind.”</i><br><br>Or….<br><br><i>“Let me get this straight,” he said, and I could tell he was laughing. <b>“You dragged Eddie to Walgreens to help pick out condoms for me?”</b> <br>“Well, I didn’t know! I’m not the kind of girl who keeps condoms around. That’s the guy’s job and you said we were gonna have to use different precautions.”<br>“Did you tell Eddie the part about long-lasting reliability?”</i>
</blockquote><br>Seriously she is a hoot and mix in a drag queen neighbor, Vietnam Vet, a car chase, a few kidnappings, a bag of diamonds and a creepy drug pin and what else do you need for a good time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287575i/17673740._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="485" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then there is Lee Nightingale, FINALLY we meet. In all the other KA reading I’ve done in the last three months he has popped up quite a few places with cameos. So I was so excited to meet him. Sure he is a KA alpha which means bossy, arrogant, hot, sexy, pushy, fantastic in bed etc…. you get the picture. But that also means that he gets moments of being sweet. What I really love about Indy and Lee is that they are so different the fit together perfectly. He is planning, control and protection while<b> Indy is Calamity, chaos</b> and affection (in a good way). Together they totally make sense and I loved that she had known him since childhood it made their romantic relationship even better.<br><br><b>General KA disclaimer</b> - I seriously feel like I have to give this to every one of her series that I love. It doesn’t make sense, either you are going to love the OOT craziness of it or you are going to hate everything about this book. I seem to almost always fall on the side of love with KA but she is just my kind of crazy it seems.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17487667573144310866" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1495817755" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1495817755" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1495817755?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1495817755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10972601140324382871">This book is NSFW, or even NSFPR (not safe for public reading). Not because of inappropriate pics, but because you will laugh so hard that people will assume you are crazy. It could be helpful on public transportation - having some space to yourself and all.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452121295i/17650070._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Hey, are you reading Rock Chick?</i><br/><br/>When I first heard about it, I was assuming it was about some girl in a band, or a girl chasing a guy in a band. Not my thing. But, it isn't at all. It is a very funny story about a girl who has been in love wi</span>
  <span id="freeText10972601140324382871" style="display:none">This book is NSFW, or even NSFPR (not safe for public reading). Not because of inappropriate pics, but because you will laugh so hard that people will assume you are crazy. It could be helpful on public transportation - having some space to yourself and all.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452121295i/17650070._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Hey, are you reading Rock Chick?</i><br><br>When I first heard about it, I was assuming it was about some girl in a band, or a girl chasing a guy in a band. Not my thing. But, it isn't at all. It is a very funny story about a girl who has been in love with her best friend's brother since she was 5, and he finally wants to get together with her. She is also in grave danger because her coffee barista got her shot at, kidnapped 3 times, stun gunned, and the attention of a small-time mobster who looks like Grandpa Munster.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452121295i/17650071.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>you'll always sparkle to me, sexy!</i><br><br>So our hero is Indy, a girl who owns a bookstore that doesn't sell many books but gets customers in through having her own coffee guy. He's an artist. Unfortunately, the artist has a side-job that involves marijuana, and said job has put him in some hot water which he immediately uses to make steam and make a kitty cat face in a caramel half-caff soy venti skinny cappuccino. And, he drags Indy into his problems.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452121295i/17650072._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> yes, I'm aware that I probably said something wrong in the fictional coffee order. I admit that I don't drink that vile bitter weed juice...</i><br><br>Lee is the boy Indy has always loved. And, her bff's brother. They have plotted and schemed for Indy and Lee to get married since they were children - all in vain. But, Lee's all grown up now, and he finally admits that he sees Indy as more than his kid sister's friend. Also, he's a badass who decides to help her with her problem. Nobody is quite sure what Lee does, but they know he does something manly and brave, and there is even a secret bedroom in his apartment that is always locked. They call it Command Center. Lucky for Indy, she is now in the inner circle (meaning she's staying at his place):<br><br><b>
  <i>I walked out of the bedroom to make coffee and stopped dead, staring at the Command Center door, which was open.<br>I expected that Lee was gone, off for a run, off to command mercenary troops in a drug war in Peru, off to put tracking devices on my car.<br>Instead I heard him talking on the phone like it was an everyday room and not the nerve center for an international commando cartel.</i>
</b><br><br>In Indy's eyes, though, it's too late for her and Lee. She spent too much of her life being rebuffed and humiliated by him. She's done with all of that.<br><br><b>
  <i>"you're like my older brother."<br>"Is that why you tried to stick your tongue down my throat when you were fifteen?"<br>Yikes.<br>"And sixteen?"<br>Crap.<br>"And seventeen?"<br>"Okay, okay, I get it. Jeez." I broke into his trip down memory lane.</i>
</b><br><br>Alright, but I can tell what you are thinking. So far this sounds like any modern chick-lit romance novel. And, you might be right. I don't read too many of those books. But still, this book is super funny. The hilarious situations, witty banter, and crazy characters make it LOL material for sure.<br><br>Indy has a bff named Ally and the two of them are like Lucy and Ethel with crazy capers. I love how they are together. Right after Indy takes out a hitman who was going towards Ally and they have the bad guys on the couch:<br><br>Eddie (cop friend) to Lee: <b>
  <i>"We gotta talk. Do you think Betty and Veronica here can keep an eye on these two?"<br>"I get to be Veronica," Ally said instantly.<br>I turned to her. "Why do you get to be Veronica?"<br>I didn't want to be Betty, Betty was a doormat. Veronica had attitude.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452122173i/17650157.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And, theirs was not the only great relationship. Indy's neighbors were a gay couple that are hilarious and awesome. I felt like the gay male friend role was written really well. I've had so many gay male friends (including my brother), and my daughter had a gay male best friend, and the author really nailed the fun and closeness of the relationship between fag and hag.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452121295i/17650074.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> the REAL definition! </i><br><br>But, all the supporting characters were awesome. The story was awesome. The book was awesome. Everything was just awesome. Read it!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452121295i/17650075.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10972601140324382871" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_267007843" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/267007843" />
    <a title="Ana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1316580-ana"><img alt="Ana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491291179p2/1316580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/267007843?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ana" href="/user/show/1316580-ana">Ana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1316580-ana?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1316580-ana?shelf=zz-read-in-2012">zz-read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer267007843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2060048590018829480">After finishing Ms. Ashley's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/69391-colorado-mountain' rel='nofollow noopener'>Colorado Mountain series</a> as well as <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13340040.Heaven_and_Hell__Heaven_and_Hell___1_' title='Heaven and Hell (Heaven and Hell, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heaven and Hell</a> I was impressed with the stories (even with the editing and some pretty convoluted sentences), so I decide to try Rock Chic series. I'm happy to say I'm not disappointed. <br/><br/>A couple reviewers compared the books to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2384.Janet_Evanovich' title='Janet Evanovich' rel='nofollow noopener'>Janet Evanovich</a>'s Stephanie Plum series and I can see the similarities. We have a clueless heroine that's been dragged into the criminal world, a handsome, extremely dangerous guy who owns a security company</span>
  <span id="freeText2060048590018829480" style="display:none">After finishing Ms. Ashley's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/69391-colorado-mountain" rel="nofollow noopener">Colorado Mountain series</a> as well as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13340040.Heaven_and_Hell__Heaven_and_Hell___1_" title="Heaven and Hell (Heaven and Hell, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Heaven and Hell</a> I was impressed with the stories (even with the editing and some pretty convoluted sentences), so I decide to try Rock Chic series. I'm happy to say I'm not disappointed. <br /><br />A couple reviewers compared the books to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2384.Janet_Evanovich" title="Janet Evanovich" rel="nofollow noopener">Janet Evanovich</a>'s Stephanie Plum series and I can see the similarities. We have a clueless heroine that's been dragged into the criminal world, a handsome, extremely dangerous guy who owns a security company (sounds familiar anyone? :-) ). So if you liked Stephanie, you'll adore Indy.<br /><br />Indy's a cop's daughter that inherited a bookstore from her grandmother.<br /><br />She's happy with her life, and then somehow everything goes to hell. Her barista managed to loose millions of dollars worth of diamonds. How stupid do you have to be?<br /><br />Her long-time crush Lee seems to be pretty focused on getting her to bed (after all this time, he thinks now is an ideal moment?)<br /><br />And she keeps waking up with him, what's up with that?<br /><br />And let's not forget all the criminals who think she knows where the diamonds are. Yay!<br /><br />I liked the book, there were lots of LOL moments. Lee's family is insane, and Indy's father as well. And then there's all the people they meet, there's not a sane person in sight. Speaking of crazy persons, I love Tex - her new (completely insane) barista. <br /><br />Lee's so deliciously dark and brooding. He's found his perfect mate in a tiny bit wacky Indy. After all, nobody else could put up with her. I love this quote:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Your grandmother used to say that you were two souls separated in heaven. She mainly meant you were both trouble and deserved each other.” </i>
</blockquote><br />He's a man with a scary reputation, but still saving Indy from herself takes a lot of effort. I love him. :D And his employees, yummy... ;-) <br /><br />I liked how Indy <b>tried</b> to stay out of the mess when guns made their appearance. It's a nice change from the TSTL heroines, with no sense of self preservation. Of course, her common sense didn't always manage to overrule her curiosity, so she did have some TSTL moments that annoyed me, but overall she was good.<br /><br />As I already mentioned in other reviews of Ms. Ashley's books, I love her characters. This book is no exception. The entire gang is hilarious and likable. I'm looking forward to reading more about them in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7405450.Rock_Chick_Rescue__Rock_Chick___2_" title="Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick Rescue</a>.<br /><br />Rating:<br /><br /><b>4 stars</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2060048590018829480" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_668223765" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668223765" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/668223765?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940011222474" href="/book/show/12437973-rock-chick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668223765" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18033657987951075604">3.5 Stars<br/><br/>This was a lot of zany fun. I do love a romance of unrequited love, but many years wasted bums me out. Lee and Indy could've been together so long before she was thirty, but for reasons I don't really buy or get, they weren't. I did like Indy and Allie's free spirit, having the most amount of fun possible, but sometimes the recklessness got to me. I think I'd have strangled Indy a few times if I were Lee. Still, good times, but definitely not my favorite Kristen Ashley.<br/><br/>On a side note, T</span>
  <span id="freeText18033657987951075604" style="display:none">3.5 Stars<br /><br />This was a lot of zany fun. I do love a romance of unrequited love, but many years wasted bums me out. Lee and Indy could've been together so long before she was thirty, but for reasons I don't really buy or get, they weren't. I did like Indy and Allie's free spirit, having the most amount of fun possible, but sometimes the recklessness got to me. I think I'd have strangled Indy a few times if I were Lee. Still, good times, but definitely not my favorite Kristen Ashley.<br /><br />On a side note, Tex was hilarious, and the secondary cast was all kinds of fun, too! <br /><br />Also, the narration was wonderful! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18033657987951075604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17616929317393792678"> <b> 5 Diamond Stars!!</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433508ra/872402.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Indy and Lee know each other since they are kids. They lived in opposite sides of the street, her dad and his parents were best friends and Indy and Ally, Lee’s younger sisters, are best friends since they’re babies. <br/>Indy had a crush on Lee for many years, but he always turned her down and one day he told him that she would always be his little sister best friend, therefore, nothing could happen between the two of them <br/>Indy feels broken, humiliated and knows this is the last </span>
  <span id="freeText17616929317393792678" style="display:none"> <b> 5 Diamond Stars!!</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433508ra/872402.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Indy and Lee know each other since they are kids. They lived in opposite sides of the street, her dad and his parents were best friends and Indy and Ally, Lee’s younger sisters, are best friends since they’re babies. <br>Indy had a crush on Lee for many years, but he always turned her down and one day he told him that she would always be his little sister best friend, therefore, nothing could happen between the two of them <br>Indy feels broken, humiliated and knows this is the last time she will try anything. From that day on, she gave up on her dream of being with Lee. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433508ra/872403.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ten years passed, during which she was able to basically avoid Lee in every party or family reunion (basically a LOT of them!) and move on and meet other people. In that time Indy stayed loyal to her rock chick lifestyle and Lee became a badass and no one knows exactly what he does. So, when one of Indy’s friends gets in trouble over some stolen diamonds, Lee is the person who she has to turn to, in order to save his friend, and herself. Ans he takes the task with pleasure… maybe too much. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798937i/647717.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You see, the thing is: Indy never really got over Lee, and he had his own reasons to turn her down, being his little sisters best friend not one of them. And not being interested in her was absolutely not another reason. (You’ll have to read it to know more.)<br>And since he was looking for an opportunity to finally have her… well, this came as the perfect excuse. Even when she says that she doesn’t want him anymore, which he don’t believe, because… let’s be real: Who the hell wouldn’t want sexy alpha-male Lee?? <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401265ra/778591.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like any other Kristen Ashley book, this was awesome.<br>We had a hilarious and strong heroine, a sexy as all hell alpha- male hero, real great supportive characters, who I can’t wait to read their books and a sexy, fun and very sweet story. Go read this series, now ;) </span>

<div id="review_829532814" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/829532814" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/829532814?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940011222474" href="/book/show/12437973-rock-chick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=jackass-heroes">jackass-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=lol-funny">lol-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=drama-rama-bo-bama">drama-rama-bo-bama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=bitchy-heroine">bitchy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=hells-yeah-alphas">hells-yeah-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=love-hate-relationship">love-hate-relationship</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer829532814" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15680114413327006295"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390415201ra/8208811.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“Your grandmother used to say that you were two souls separated in heaven. She mainly meant you were both trouble and deserved each other.” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>I can't believe I hadn't read this one before now. This book was slightly different than the other books I've read from Kristen Ashley. There was a lot more humour in this one, which I really enjoyed.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Indy Savage is the daughter of a cop,</span>
  <span id="freeText15680114413327006295" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390415201ra/8208811.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Your grandmother used to say that you were two souls separated in heaven. She mainly meant you were both trouble and deserved each other.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I can't believe I hadn't read this one before now. This book was slightly different than the other books I've read from Kristen Ashley. There was a lot more humour in this one, which I really enjoyed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Indy Savage is the daughter of a cop, a bookstore owner, and a wild child. She's loved Lee Nightingale since she was five years old. Once she was old enough, she would practically throw herself at him, only to be rejected. After feeling humilitated by the last rejection, she made sure to avoid him for good and move on. Now she's in trouble because of her coffee 'artiste' Rosie who apparently has some diamonds these men want. He has dealt pot to the wrong people and now they seem to be after him, which in turn means her too. How do they know? They get shot at. The only one who can help them is the one she wants to keep at arms lengths, Lee.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390419263i/8209459._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“He’s good at this stuff.”<br>“What stuff?”<br>“Relationship stuff. He’s a natural. It’s weird, we’re new and we’re old. I can’t get my head around it.”<br>“He’s shit at relationship stuff. He’s only good at it because it’s you.”<br>“Sorry?”<br>“You’re shit at it too, but only because it was never him.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Indy was this crazy rock chick. She was fun and outgoing. I felt for her when it came to her feeling totally embarrassed from the last rejection she got from Lee. They have grown up together, so they have been and still are in each others lives because of family events. But when he tells her she is like his little sister (OUCH!), she gives up on him and tries to move on with other guys. Indy was quite badass, but not in crazy manly proportions. I loved that about her, she and her best friend were also kind of fearless. But she was annoying in a few scenes. She would have these tantrums that were a tad childish for a thirty year old. But overall, I liked her.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390419175i/8209437._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“For what it’s worth, I’ll share my intentions. You and me, we aren’t practice for the real thing. It isn’t that too much is at stake with family and friends, it’s because I love you. You’re funny, beautiful and you care about people. I like the way you look at me, especially when you think I don’t notice it. I like that we have history and our kids will have a big family and share that history because there was never a time when their Mom and Dad weren’t together. If you were a terrible lay, I might have second thoughts but you and I are dynamite together. I intend to marry you and spend the rest of my life with you. If that freaks you out, tough, because now we’ve started this, there’s no goin’ back.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Lee Nightingale is well... who the hell knows. But he is an alpha badass and has a command center, nuff said. Lee has wanted Indy for quite some time. But he was waiting for his moment where they would both be more stable and not crazy hormone ridden teens. Unfortunately, Indy has been avoiding him for a decade. Now, he has a chance with her and he isn't giving it up. He will do anything to protect her *sigh*, and anything to have her. I will admit, I was not impressed by him in the beginning. He came off as a total A-hole and he could be too blunt. But as I kept reading, he grew on me. Plus, he was really sexy and delicious, so it wasn't hard.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Just a little pointer, Indy, girl to girl, if you want that week with Lee to last into two. He likes it when you go down on him in the morning. He’s a fucking animal in bed but give him a morning BJ, he’ll return the favor and rock your world.”<br>Every muscle in my body froze solid.<br>“What did she just say?” Stevie asked.<br>“She did not just say that in front of me,” Kitty Sue said.<br>“Holy crap,” Dolores said.<br>“Oh… my… gawd,” Tod said.<br>“You fucking bitch,” Ally said.<br>“This is more like it,” Tex said.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>All the characters were actually quite entertaining. Rosie was freaking weird but at times really funny. The Kevster, who was a stoner was freaking hilarious. He made me laugh out loud many times. But not as much as Tex the loony cat man. He was a freaking hoot! Ally was an awesome best friend but a little to out there and just as stubborn as Indy. Tod (The drag queen) and Stevie were also such great characters that I enjoyed.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>In his ear, really quietly, I whispered, "I'm not going anywhere. I'm right where I've always wanted to be."<br><br>His mouth moved to mind and he said, "It's about fucking time."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This book had some action, some quite hilarious moments, a bit of steam (nothing too crazy hot), and of course some sexy alpha badass men. I totally forgot to mention that these two, were interrupted SO many times throughout the book while they were 'trying' to get it on. I felt their pain, hahaha! It was a fun read and really entertaining. All of the characters were a bunch of oddballs but together they were all perfect and the banter was just awesome. There were a few moments however, that I felt the story dragged on a bit, which had me skimming. These were just a few parts throughout the book. I did really, <i>really</i> liked Lee...but didn't end up loving him. I didn't like why he waited so long and his reasons for being a jerk. Stil, l liked him nonetheless, even if he was a possessive caveman at times. It was a great book, may not be a top Kristen Ashley book for me, but really freaking great. One you should definitely give a try. I can't wait to read Eddie's book *sigh*. He had me <i>very</i> interested from this book that I can't wait to read his very soon. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15680114413327006295" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1941265646" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8719649530693508505">🎉 <i>PSA: this book is on sale aus kindle, AND THIS SERIES IS THE BEST (22/06/19)</i>. <br/><br/><b>4.5/5 stars</b> <br/><br/><b>reread:</b> <br/>18/05/17<br/>13/05/18<br/>01/06/19<br/><br/><i>reread comment: this will always be one of my favourite Rock Chick books, you can never beat the OG couple who brought all the crazy and wonderful characters together. I love everything about this book, Ally & Indy's relationship, the best friend's older brother crush trope and how freaking bomb Kitty Sue is. The most under appreciated character in this series has to be Kit</i></span>
  <span id="freeText8719649530693508505" style="display:none">🎉 <i>PSA: this book is on sale aus kindle, AND THIS SERIES IS THE BEST (22/06/19)</i>. <br /><br /><b>4.5/5 stars</b> <br /><br /><b>reread:</b> <br />18/05/17<br />13/05/18<br />01/06/19<br /><br /><i>reread comment: this will always be one of my favourite Rock Chick books, you can never beat the OG couple who brought all the crazy and wonderful characters together. I love everything about this book, Ally &amp; Indy's relationship, the best friend's older brother crush trope and how freaking bomb Kitty Sue is. The most under appreciated character in this series has to be Kitty Sue, that mamma is amazing and I adore her.</i><br /><br />This book follows Indy Savage, bookstore owner, rock chick and all round badass. Indy has been in love with her best friend's brother and family friend Lee, since she was five. And she spent the next fifteen years attempting to catch him. After a particularly bad rebuff, Indy gives up all hope and attempts to avoid Lee's very existence for the next ten years. <br /><br />Until trouble begins to follow Indy, and Lee (being the owner of the best PI firm in Denver and an all around badass) is the only person who can protect her. Turns out, he's hell bent on protecting her.<br /><br />This book is a whole lot of angst, drama and action. And when I say drama, this book takes that whole concept to a whole new entertaining level. The characters were all adorable and like KA does best, the most wonderful smorgasbord of crazy characters imaginable. Their whole little group take on a life of their own, and no matter how many times I've read this book <i>(which is a fair few by now),</i> they'll always be some of my favourite. <br /><br />There was a family and community vibe that ran strong through this book which I loved, and the relationship between Lee and Indy was full of drama, excitement and adorable moments. Lee and Indy will always have a special place in my heart as the first couple in this wonderful series. <br /><br /><b>my reviews and ratings for <i>Kristen Ashely's</i> other books:</b><br />• <a   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8TCI/3n/Y+xMtmPkhEjmbiQpmIcowdmpE0L0UiTQYrRcsJjp7y5W44Yxj2tovhDFTgOTFkjfMkCypEFdD38Nmw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S248r84H7ZRfa/Nli4K5JPfsd3TDAcHGOXw1/em4EnXm7iy5WNbYm5XsH+pndE+PncZ85aMfKi+YmoDywhd9Wg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText10383887323274086685" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
